Jamison Brereton

47 (667)
A╠Дdityas
Trita ─Аptya
18 verses: mah─Бpaс╣Еkti
The first two-thirds of this hymn (through vs. 12) beg the ─Аdityas for general help and protection from generic evilsтАФthe nonspecific nature of what is requested underlined by the rather redundantly phrased refrain. The refrain continues through the last third of the hymn (vss. 13тАУ18), but in the non-refrain portions the focus nar
rowsтАФto the elimination of the тАЬbad dream,тАЭ which is sent far away to the shadowy figure called Trita ─Аptya. Nothing else in the scraps of mythology we know about Trita ─Аptya explains why he should be the scapegoated recipient of our nightmares, much less why he would make them into body ornaments (vs. 15) or use them as food and work (vs. 16). The agent who removes the bad dream to Trita is Dawn (vss. 14тАУ16, 18), whose participation is easier to understandтАФas anyone knows who has experienced the relief of waking in the morning to discover that the nightmares just experienced were not real.

Jamison Brereton Notes

─Аdityas

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬMitra and Varuс╣Зa, you are great, and great is your protection to the offerer; no evil, ─Аdityas, harmshim whom you guard from the injurer; your aids are void of harm, your aids are true aids.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Great is the help, of (all of) you who are great, for the pious man, o Varuс╣Зa and Mitra.
Whomever you protect from deceit, o ─Аdityas, evil will not reach him. тАУ Your help is faultless; very helpful is your help.

Jamison Brereton Notes

Although only Mitra and Varuс╣Зa are mentioned in the first hemistich, vo mahat─Б╠Бm is gen. pl. and must refer to all the ─Аdityas, who are addressed in the next clause (p─Бda c).

Griffith

GREAT help ye give the worshipper, Varuna, Mitra, Mighty Ones! No sorrow ever reaches him whom ye, Adityas, keep from harm. Yours are incomparable aids, and good the succour they afford.

Geldner

Gro├Я ist euer, der Gro├Яen, Schutz, o Varuna, Mitra, f├╝r den Opferspender. Wen ihr Aditya┬┤s vor Arglist sch├╝tzet, den trifft kein ├Ьbel. - Ohne Fehler sind eure Hilfen, guthelfend sind eure Hilfen.

Grassmann

Ihr grossen reichet grossen Schutz dem Frommen, Mitra-Varuna; Wen ihr Aditja’s vor Gefahr besch├╝tzet, den erreicht kein Leid; ganz unvergleichlich ist eur Schutz, und herrlich schirmend euer Schirm.

Elizarenkova

English translation:

тАЬDivine ─Аdityas, you know the averting of evils; as birds (spread) their wings over (their) young, grantus happiness; your aids are void of harm, your aids are true aids.тАЭ

You know how to make evils stay away, o gods, o ─Аdityas.
Like birds their wings, spread your shelter out above us.
тАУ Your help is faultless; very helpful is your help.

O Gods, Adityas, well ye know the way to keep all woes afar.
As the birds spread their sheltering wings, spread your protection over us.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬGrant us that happiness of yours, as birds (spread) their wings; O you possessed of all wealth, wesolicit all riches suitable for our dwelling; your aids are void of harm, your aids are true aids.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Spread that shelter out over us, like birds their wings.
We revere all things providing defense, o you who possess all
possessions.
тАУ Your help is faultless; very helpful is your help.

Griffith

As the birds spread their sheltering wings let your protection cover us.
We mean all shelter and defence, ye who have all things for your own.

Geldner

Spannet ├╝ber uns diesen Schirm aus, wie V├╢gel die Fl├╝gel! Alle Schutzmittel haben wir im Sinne, ihr Allwissende. - Ohne Fehler sind eure Hilfen, guthelfend sind eure Hilfen.

Grassmann

Den Schutz verbreitet ├╝ber uns, wie V├╢gel ihrer Fl├╝gel Paar; Ja, alles, was uns schirmen kann, allwissende erflehen wir; ganz unvergleichlich ist eur Schutz und herrlich schirmend euer Schirm.

Elizarenkova

рдпрд╕реНрдореИ рдордиреБрд╖реНрдпрд╛рдп рдХреНрд╖рдпрдВ рдирд┐рд╡рд╛рд╕рдВ рдЬреАрд╡рд╛рддреБрдВ рдЬреАрд╡рдирд╕рд╛рдзрдирдордиреНрдирдВ рдЪ рдкреНрд░рдЪреЗрддрд╕рдГ рдкреНрд░рдХреГрд╖реНрдЯрдорддрдпрдГ рдЕрд░рд╛рд╕рдд рдкреНрд░рдпрдЪреНрдЫрдиреНрддрд┐ рддрд╕реНрдореИ рдпрдЬрдорд╛рдирд╛рдп рддрджрд░реНрдердореН рдЗрдореЗ рдЖрджрд┐рддреНрдпрд╛рдГ рд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡рд╕реНрдп рдШреЗрддреН рд╕рд░реНрд╡рд╕реНрдпрд╛рдкреНрдпрдпрд╖реНрдЯреБрдГ рдордиреЛрдГ рдордиреБрд╖реНрдпрд╕реНрдп рдзрдирд┐рдХрд╕реНрдп рд░рд╛рдпрдГ рдзрдирд╕реНрдп рдИрд╢рддреЗ рд╕реНрд╡рд╛рдорд┐рдиреЛ рднрд╡рдиреНрддреНрдпрдкрд╣реГрддреНрдп рдпрдЬрдорд╛рдирд╛рдп рдкреНрд░рджрд╛рддреБрдореН рее

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬTo whomsoever these wise ─Аdityas gran a dwelling and the means of life, (for him) they master thewealth of every man; your aids are void of harm, your aids are true aids.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Of every man: who does not offersacrifice

Jamison Brereton

MankindтАФto which the attentive ones gave peaceful dwelling and livelihoodтАФ
over all its wealth do these ─Аdityas hold sway.
тАУ Your help is faultless; very helpful is your help.

Griffith

To whomsoever they, Most Wise, have given a home and means of life,
O’er the whole riches of this man they, the Adityas, have control.

Geldner

Wem die F├╝rsorglichen Wohnung und Lebensunterhalt gew├дhrt haben - diese Aditya┬┤s verf├╝gen ja ├╝ber den ganzen Reichtum des Menschen. - Ohne Fehler sind eure Hilfen, guthelfend sind eure Hilfen.

Grassmann

Wem sie, die weisen, sichern Sitz und Lebensunterhalt verliehn, Des Menschen ganzer Reichthum steht in ihrer, der Aditja’s, Hand; ganz unvergleichlich ist eur Schutz und herrlich schirmend euer Schirm.

Elizarenkova

рдкрджрд╛рд░реНрдерд╛рдиреНрд╡рдпрднрд╛рд╖рд╛рдГ - (рд╡рд░реБрдг) рд╣реЗ рд╡рд░рдгреАрдп рд░рд╛рдЬрдкреНрд░рддрд┐рдирд┐рдзреЗ (рдорд┐рддреНрд░) рд╣реЗ рдмреНрд░рд╛рд╣реНрдордгрдкреНрд░рддрд┐рдирд┐рдзреЗ рд╣реЗ рдЕрдиреНрдпрд╛рдиреНрдп рд╢реНрд░реЗрд╖реНрда рдорд╛рдирд╡рдЧрдг ! English translation:

тАЬMay our sins avoid us as charioteers inaccessible plural ce; may we abide in Indra’s happiness and in theprotection of the ─Аdiyas; your aids are void of harm, your aids are true aids.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Evils will avoid us, as charioteers avoid hard places.
Might we be in the shelter of Indra and the help of the ─Аdityas.
тАУ Your help is faultless; very helpful is your help.

Jamison Brereton Notes

The simile is slightly skewed, though, as in English, the case frame with тАШavoidтАЩ works either way. It might be expected that тАЬweтАЭ would be compared to the (presumably) nominative rathy├ас╕е тАШcharioteersтАЩ, but grammatically тАЬweтАЭ are parallel to the hard places (durg─Б╠Бс╣Зi). Of course technically both durg─Б╠Бс╣Зi and rathy├ас╕е can be either nom. or acc. pl., so that the skewing could be avoided: тАЬEvils will avoid us, as hard places avoid charioteers.тАЭ But this produces an unintentionally comic picture, and I follow Geldner and Renou in the case distribution.

Griffith

As drivers of the car avoid ill roads, let sorrows pass us by.
May we be under Indra’s guard, in the Adityas’ favouring grace.

Geldner

Uns sollen die ├Ьbel meiden wie Wagenlenker die schlimmen Wege. Wir m├╢chten unter dem Schirm des Indra und in dem Schutz der Aditya┬┤s sein. - Ohne Fehler sind eure Hilfen, guthelfend sind eure Hilfen.

Grassmann

Gefahren m├╢gen meiden uns, wie Wagenlenker ├╝blen Weg; Wir m├╢gen sein in Indra’s Hut und recht in der Aditja’s Schutz; ganz unvergleichlich ist eur Schutz und herrlich schirmend euer Schirm.

Elizarenkova

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬOnly by painful means does a living man obtain the wealth which you bestow; but he whom you, divine─Аdityas, visit, wins great (riches); your aids are void of harm, your aids are true aids.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

By painful means = bypenance, religious observances; a living ma: ana = pr─Бс╣Зa-yuktaс╕е, endowed with life; (RV 4.30.3):pr─Бс╣Зar┼лpena balena; or, just a particle, ‘certainly’; verily men succumb through the loss of the wealth given byyou?; ─Б┼Ыa vaс╕е = ─Б┼Ыavaс╕е, swiftly moving

Jamison Brereton

It is only by a crooked course that in such a way a man becomes lost to what is given by you.
O gods, o ─Аdityas, itтАЩs not a trifle that he obtained from youтАФthe man whom you spurred on.
тАУ Your help is faultless; very helpful is your help.

Jamison Brereton Notes

This verse is contrastively complementary to the preceding one. Both p├бri тИЪvс╣Ыj and p├бri тИЪhvс╣Ы mean тАШswerve, turn aside, avoidтАЩ, but in vs. 5 p├бri тАж vс╣Ыс╣Зajan is a beneficial action, whereas here parihvс╣Ыt─Б╠Б(on accent see Oldenberg, Scarlatta 708) refers to turning aside from the proper course, an action that causes a man to lose out on the ─АdityasтАЩ gift. How substantial this gift can be for someone whom the ─Аdityas favor is expressed in cd.

Griffith

For verily men sink and faint through loss of wealth which ye have given.
Much hath he gained from you, O Gods, whom ye, Adityas, have approached.

Geldner

Durch diesen R├дnkespinner kommt man um das von euch geschenkte Gut. Ihr G├╢tter, nicht zu wenig hat er von euch erlangt, den ihr Aditya┬┤s angespornt habt. - Ohne Fehler sind eure Hilfen, guthelfend sind eure Hilfen.

Grassmann

Denn durch Betrug verliert der Mensch das Gut, das ihr ihm habt verliehn, O G├╢tter, viel erlangt von euch, wem hold ihr, o Aditja’s, seid; ganz unvergleichlich ist eur Schutz und herrlich schirmend euer Schirm.

Elizarenkova

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬHim fierce wrath touches not, nor heavy (calamity), to whom, ─Аdityas, you have given greathappiness; your aids are void of harm, your aids are true aids.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Fierce wrath: tigmam: him, though fierce (orharsh) wrath touches not; you have iven great happiness: saprathas: neuter nominative singular agreeing with ┼Ыarma

Jamison Brereton

Negligence, sharp or weighty, will never beset him
to whom you, ─Аdityas, have given broad shelter.
тАУ Your help is faultless; very helpful is your help.

Griffith

On him shall no fierce anger fall, no sore distress shall visit him,
To whom, Adityas, ye have lent your shelter that extendeth far.

Geldner

Weder heftige noch schwere Schuld wird den ereilen, dem ihr Aditya┬┤s euren Schirm in ganzer Breite gew├дhrt habt. - Ohne Fehler sind eure Hilfen, guthelfend sind eure Hilfen.

Grassmann

Und den ereilt kein scharf Geschoss, noch st├╝rzt auf den ein wuchtiges, Wem ihr, Aditja’s, weiten Schirm und sichern Schutz verliehen habt; ganz unvergleichlich ist eur Schutz und herrlich schirmend euer Schirm.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬMay Aditi defend us, may Aditi grant us happiness, the mother of the wealthy Mitra, Aryama andVaruс╣Зa; your aids are void of harm, your aids are true aids.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

Let Aditi deliver us; let Aditi spread her shelterтАФ
the mother of rich Mitra, of Aryaman and Varuс╣Зa.
тАУYour help is faultless; very helpful is your help.

Jamison Brereton Notes

Geldner and Renou take rev├бtaс╕е with Aryaman, not Mitra. It is true that the adj. is positioned between the two names and could in principle modify either one or both, but it belongs to the same p─Бda as mitr├бsya, and the following p─Бda containing aryamс╣З├бс╕е is a repeated p─Бda (=I.136.2e), in a verse where rev├бnt- is not found. Since, further, rev├бnt- is not a standard epithet of Aryaman, it seems wise to take it with Mitra.

Griffith

May Aditi defend us, may Aditi guard and shelter us,
Mother of wealthy Mitra and of Aryaman and Varuna.

Geldner

Aditi soll uns frei machen, Aditi soll ihren Schirm gew├дhren, die Mutter des Mitra, des reichen Aryaman und des Varuna. - Ohne Fehler sind eure Hilfen, guthelfend sind eure Hilfen.

Grassmann

Es gebe Raum uns Aditi, und Aditi verleih uns Schutz, Des reichen Mitra Mutter sie, des Arjaman und Varuna; ganz unvergleichlich ist eur Schutz und herrlich schirmend euer Schirm.

Elizarenkova

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬGrant to us, deities, that happiness which is a refuge, auspicious, and free from sickness, which isthreefold and fit for a (secure) shelter; your aids are void of harm, your aids are true aids.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Threefold: tridh─Бtu =protecing against cold, heat and wind or wet (RV 8.18.21, trivar┼лtha); or, simply three elements

Jamison Brereton

That sheltering shelter, o gods, beneficial and without damage,
providing threefold defenseтАФspread that out over us.
тАУ Your help is faultless; very helpful is your help.

Jamison Brereton Notes

I have not rendered the four nominal y├бd clauses, the last three of which merely introduce further adjectival qualifiers of ┼Ы├бrma. The configuration is perilously close to an izafe-type construction, though syntactially nominal clauses are perfectly workable.

Griffith

The shelter, Gods, that is secure, auspicious, free from malady,
A sure protection, triply strong, even that do ye extend to us.

Geldner

Den sch├╝tzenden Schirm, o G├╢tter, den heilsamen, gesundmachenden, den dreifachen, beh├╝tenden, den spannet ├╝ber uns aus! - Ohne Fehler sind eure Hilfen, guthelfend sind eure Hilfen.

Grassmann

Welch Schutz, o G├╢tter, schirmend ist und heilbegabt und unversehrt, Der dreifach uns beh├╝ten kann, den reichet uns, den breitet aus; ganz unvergleichlich ist eur Schutz und herrlich schirmend euer Schirm.

Elizarenkova

тАЬ─Аdityas, look down upon us as those who look from the shore; as (men lead) their horses to a secureGh─Бс╣нa, so conduct us along a good path; your aids are void of harm, your aids are void of harm, your aids aretrue aids.тАЭ

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬLet there not be prosperit here to our powerul (foe), nor to him who threaten or assails us; but let therebe prosperity to our cattle, our kine, and our male offspring desirous of food; your aids are void of harm, your aidsare true aids.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Nor to him who threatens or assails us: neither to threaten nor to assail us

Jamison Brereton

There is no benefit for the demonic here, for him to descend and to come near.
There is benefit for the milk-giving cow and for the hero seeking fame. тАУ Your help is faultless; very helpful is your help.

Griffith

Ill be it for the demons’ friend to find us or come near to us.
But for the milch-cow be it well, and for the man who strives for fame.

Geldner

рд╣реЗ рджреЗрд╡рд╛рд╕рдГ рджреЗрд╡рд╛ рдЖрджрд┐рддреНрдпрд╛рдГ рдпрджрд╛рд╡рд┐рдГ рдпрддреН рдкрд╛рдкрдорд╛рд╡рд┐рд░реНрднреВрддрдореН рдЕрд╕реНрддрд┐ ред рджреБрд╖реНрдХреГрддрдВ рдпрддреН рдЪ рдЕрдкреАрдЪреНрдпрдореН рдЕрдиреНрддрд░реНрд╣рд┐рддрдорд╕реНрддрд┐ ред тАШ рдЕрдкреАрдЪреНрдпрдореН’ рдЗрддреНрдпрдиреНрддрд░реНрд╣рд┐рддрдирд╛рдо ред рддрджреНрд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡рдВ рддрджреБрднрдпрдореН рдЖрдкреНрддреНрдпреЗ рддреНрд░рд┐рддреЗ рдордпрд┐ рдорд╛ рднреВрддреНред рдХрд┐рдВрддреБ рдЕрд╕реНрдорддреН рдЖрд░реЗ рджреВрд░реЗ рджрдзрд╛рддрди рд╕реНрдерд╛рдкрдпрдд рее

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬDeities, whatever evil is manifest, whatever is concealed, (let it be not found) in Trita ─Аptya, keep it farfrom us; your aids are void of harm, your aids are true aids.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Trita ─Аptya is the с╣Ыс╣гi of the hymn. Trita ─Аptyawas a deity dwelling in remote distance, and consequently evil was sought to be transferred to him; keep it farfrom us in Trita ─Аptya

Jamison Brereton

Whatever is ill-done in the open, whatever in secret, o gods,
all that set on Trita ─Аptya, far away from us.
тАУ Your help is faultless; very helpful is your help.

Griffith

Each evil deed made manifest, and that which is concealed, O Gods,
The whole thereof remove from us to Trita Aptya far away.

Geldner

Welche Missetat, ihr G├╢tter, offenkundig, welche geheim ist, all die schaffet von uns in die Ferne zu Trita Aptya! - Ohne Fehler sind eure Hilfen, guthelfend sind eure Hilfen.

Grassmann

Was offenbar, was ins Geheim, o G├╢tter, Uebles ist gethan, Das alles schaffet weit hinweg von uns zu Trita Aptia; ganz unvergleichlich ist eur Schutz und herrlich schirmend euer Schirm.

Elizarenkova

тАЬDaughter of heaven, (Uс╣гas), whatever ill-omened dream threatens our cattle, keep it, O brilliant one,far from Trita ─Аptya; y our aids are void of harm, your aids, are true aids.тАЭ

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬDaughter of heaven, whatever ill-omened dream threatens Trita ─Аptya, we transfer it to the worker ofgold ornaments or to the maker of garlands; your aids are void of harm, your aids are true aids.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Whatever evildream threatens the worker of gold ornaments or the maker of garlands, that evil, abiding in Trita ─Аptya (or theson of the waters), we Tс╣Ыtas throw off from ourselves; i.e. we throw it off on Trita ─Аptya

Jamison Brereton

He will make (it) his neck ornament or his garland, o Daughter of HeavenтАФ
the whole bad dream we consign to Trita ─Аptya.
тАУ Your help is faultless; very helpful is your help.

Jamison Brereton Notes

The accent on kс╣Ыс╣З├бvate is somewhat puzzling. Renou explains it as a reflection of the implicit subordination following on vss. 13 and 14, but perhaps better is the implicit contrast of the v─Б тАж v─Б constuction.

Griffith

Even if, O Child of Heaven, it make a garland or a chain of gold,
The whole bad dream, whate’cr it be, to Trita Aptya we consign.

Geldner

Grassmann

Legt er sich einen Halsschmuck an und Blumenkranz, o Himmelskind, zu Trita Aptia schaffen wir jedweden b├╢sen Traum hinweg.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬUс╣гas, bear (elsewhere) the ill-omened dream for Trita and Dvita, who eat and do (in dreams) that(which is eaten and done amiss when awake) and who obtain that (inauspicious) portion; your aids are void ofharm, your aids are true aids.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Bear elsewhere: i.e., let the eating of honey etc., perceived in a dream, producehappiness as in a waking state; trita and dvita: for dvita, cf. ┼Ъatapatha Br─Бhmaс╣Зa 1.2.3.1

Jamison Brereton

To the one who has it as his food and as his work, to the one reverently approaching it as his portionтАФ
to Trita and to Dvita, o Dawn, carry the bad dream.
тАУ Your help is faultless; very helpful is your help.

Griffith

To him whose food and work is this, who comes to take his share therein,
To Trita, and to Dvita, Dawn! bear thou the evil dream away.

Grassmann

Der diese Speis’ und dieses Werk gewohnt ist, diesen Antheil hat, dem Trita und dem Dvita fahr, o Uschas hin den b├╢sen Traum.

Elizarenkova

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬAs (in the sacrifice) we put severally together the proper parts and the hoofs, and as we discharge adebt, so we transfer all the ill-omened dream that rests on ─Аptya; your aids are void of harm, your aids are trueaids.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

As in the sacrifice they plural ce together the kal─Б, the heart etc., as fit to be cut to pieces, and the ┼Ыapha,the hoof, bones etc. as unfit; another explanation is: kal─Б = ┼Ыapha or hoof. The words kal─Б and ┼Ыapha occurtogether in Taittir─лya Saс╣Гhit─Б 6.1.10, where the process of buying the Soma is desscribed;

┼Ъapha = the eighthpart of a cow;

Kal─Б = a very small portion of a cow; that rests on ─Аptya: or, we transfer all the ill-omened dreamto ─Аptya

Jamison Brereton

Just as we bring back a sixteenth, then an eighth, then the
(whole) debt,
even so we bring the whole bad dream to ─Аptya.
тАУ Your help is faultless; very helpful is your help.

Griffith

As we collect the utmost debt, even the eighth and sixteenth part,
So unto Aptya we transfer together all the evil dream.

Geldner

Wie wir ein Sechzehntel, wie ein Achtel, wie wir die ganze Schuld aufbringen, so bringen wir alles b├╢se Tr├дumen zusammen auf Aptya. - Ohne Fehler sind eure Hilfen, guthelfend sind eure Hilfen.

Grassmann

Wie man die Schulden abbezahlt, den Pfennig und den Heller auch, so zahlen jeden b├╢sen Traum wir ab an Trita Aptia.

Elizarenkova

рдкрджрд╛рд░реНрдерд╛рдиреНрд╡рдпрднрд╛рд╖рд╛рдГ - рд╣реЗ рджрд┐рд╡реЛ рджреБрд╣рд┐рддрдГ ! рдкреНрд░рдХрд╛рд╢рд╕реНрдп рдХрдиреНрдпреЗ рдмреБрджреНрдзреЗ ! рдпрджреНрд╡рд╛ред рд╣реЗ рдЙрд╖рдГред рд╡рд╛=рдЕрдерд╡рд╛ред рдирд┐рд╖реНрдХрдорд╛рднрд░рдгрдореНред рдХреГрдгрд╡рддреЗ=рдХреГрддрд╡рддреЗред рд╡рд╛=рдЕрдерд╡рд╛ред рд╕реНрд░рдЬрдВ рдорд╛рд▓реНрдпрдВ рдХреГрддрд╡рддреЗред рдорд╣реНрдпрдВ рдпрджреН рджреБрдГрд╕реНрд╡рдкреНрдиреНрдпрдВ рдЬрд╛рдпрддреЗред рддрддреНрд╕рд░реНрд╡рдореНред рдЖрдкреНрддреНрдпреЗ рддреНрд░рд┐рддреЗред рдкрд░рд┐рджрджреНрдорд╕рд┐=рд╕реНрдерд╛рдкрдпрд╛рдордГ реерезрелрее
